Welcome to Abella 2.0.2-dev 
Abella < Kind name, action, proc type.

Abella < Type null proc.

Abella < Type taup proc -> proc.

Abella < Type plus, par proc -> proc -> proc.

Abella < Type match, out name -> name -> proc -> proc.

Abella < Type in name -> (name -> proc) -> proc.

Abella < Type nu (name -> proc) -> proc.

Abella < Type repl proc -> proc.

Abella < Type tau action.

Abella < Type up, dn name -> name -> action.

Abella < Type a, b name.

Abella < Define one : proc -> action -> proc -> prop,	
oneb : proc -> (name -> action) -> (name -> proc) -> prop by 
one (taup P) tau P;
one (out X Y P) (up X Y) P;
one (plus P Q) A R := one P A R;
one (plus P Q) A R := one Q A R;
one (par P Q) A (par P1 Q) := one P A P1;
one (par P Q) A (par P Q1) := one Q A Q1;
one (nu (x\P x)) A (nu (x\Q x)) := nabla x, one (P x) A (Q x);
one (par P Q) tau (nu (y\par (M y) (N y))) := exists X, oneb P (dn X) M /\ oneb Q (up X) N;
one (par P Q) tau (nu (y\par (M y) (N y))) := exists X, oneb P (up X) M /\ oneb Q (dn X) N;
one (par P Q) tau (par (M Y) T) := exists X, oneb P (dn X) M /\ one Q (up X Y) T;
one (par P Q) tau (par R (M Y)) := exists X, oneb Q (dn X) M /\ one P (up X Y) R;
one (repl P) A (par (repl P) P1) := one P A P1;
one (repl P) tau (par (par P1 (M Y)) (repl P)) := exists X, one P (up X Y) P1 /\ oneb P (dn X) M;
one (repl P) tau (par (nu (y\par (N y) (M y))) (repl P)) := exists X, oneb P (up X) N /\ oneb P (dn X) M;
oneb (in X M) (dn X) M;
oneb (plus P Q) A M := oneb P A M;
oneb (plus P Q) A M := oneb Q A M;
oneb (par P Q) A (x\par (M x) Q) := oneb P A M;
oneb (par P Q) A (x\par P (N x)) := oneb Q A N;
oneb (nu (x\P x)) A (y\nu (x\Q x y)) := nabla x, oneb (P x) A (y\Q x y);
oneb (nu (x\M x)) (up X) N := nabla y, one (M y) (up X y) (N y);
oneb (repl P) A (x\par (repl P) (M x)) := oneb P A M.

Abella < CoDefine bisim_up_to : (proc -> proc -> proc -> proc -> prop) -> proc -> proc -> prop by 
bisim_up_to Upto P Q := (forall A P1, one P A P1 -> (exists Q1, one Q A Q1 /\ (exists P2 Q2,
  Upto P1 P2 Q1 Q2 /\ bisim_up_to Upto P2 Q2))) /\ (forall X M,
  oneb P (dn X) M -> (exists N, oneb Q (dn X) N /\ (exists M2 N2, forall W,
  Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\ bisim_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))) /\
  (forall X M, oneb P (up X) M -> (exists N, oneb Q (up X) N /\
  (exists M2 N2, nabla W, Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
  bisim_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))) /\ (forall A Q1, one Q A Q1 ->
  (exists P1, one P A P1 /\ (exists P2 Q2, Upto P1 P2 Q1 Q2 /\
  bisim_up_to Upto P2 Q2))) /\ (forall X N, oneb Q (dn X) N -> (exists M,
  oneb P (dn X) M /\ (exists M2 N2, forall W,
  Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\ bisim_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))) /\
  (forall X N, oneb Q (up X) N -> (exists M, oneb P (up X) M /\
  (exists M2 N2, nabla W, Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
  bisim_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))).

Abella < Define refl_t : proc -> proc -> proc -> proc -> prop by 
refl_t P P Q Q.

Abella < Define bisim_t : proc -> proc -> proc -> proc -> prop by 
bisim_t P1 P2 Q1 Q2 := bisim_up_to refl_t P1 P2 /\ bisim_up_to refl_t Q1 Q2.

Abella < Define oneWeak : proc -> action -> proc -> prop by 
oneWeak P tau P;
oneWeak P tau P2 := exists P1, one P tau P1 /\ oneWeak P1 tau P2;
oneWeak P A P3 := (A = tau -> false) /\ (exists P1 P2, oneWeak P tau P1 /\ one P1 A P2 /\
  oneWeak P2 tau P3).

Abella < Define oneWeakb : proc -> (name -> action) -> (name -> proc) -> prop by 
oneWeakb P A P2 := exists P1, oneWeak P tau P1 /\ oneb P1 A P2.

Abella < CoDefine bisimWeak_up_to : (proc -> proc -> proc -> proc -> prop) -> proc -> proc -> prop by 
bisimWeak_up_to Upto P Q := (forall A P1, oneWeak P A P1 -> (exists Q1, oneWeak Q A Q1 /\ (exists P2 Q2,
  Upto P1 P2 Q1 Q2 /\ bisimWeak_up_to Upto P2 Q2))) /\ (forall X M,
  oneWeakb P (dn X) M -> (exists N, oneWeakb Q (dn X) N /\ (exists M2 N2,
  forall W, Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
  bisimWeak_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))) /\ (forall X M,
  oneWeakb P (up X) M -> (exists N, oneWeakb Q (up X) N /\ (exists M2 N2,
  nabla W, Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
  bisimWeak_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))) /\ (forall A Q1, oneWeak Q A Q1 ->
  (exists P1, oneWeak P A P1 /\ (exists P2 Q2, Upto P1 P2 Q1 Q2 /\
  bisimWeak_up_to Upto P2 Q2))) /\ (forall X N, oneWeakb Q (dn X) N ->
  (exists M, oneWeakb P (dn X) M /\ (exists M2 N2, forall W,
  Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\ bisimWeak_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))) /\
  (forall X N, oneWeakb Q (up X) N -> (exists M, oneWeakb P (up X) M /\
  (exists M2 N2, nabla W, Upto (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
  bisimWeak_up_to Upto (M2 W) (N2 W)))).

Abella < Define equally_structured : (proc -> proc -> prop) -> prop by 
equally_structured Pred := forall X1 X2 Y1 Y2, Pred X1 X2 -> Y1 = X1 -> Y2 = X2 -> Pred Y1 Y2.

Abella < Theorem equality_for_structured_weak : 
equally_structured (bisimWeak_up_to refl_t).



  ============================
   equally_structured (bisimWeak_up_to refl_t)

equality_for_structured_weak < unfold.



  ============================
   forall X1 X2 Y1 Y2, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t X1 X2 -> Y1 = X1 -> Y2 = X2 ->
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Y1 Y2

equality_for_structured_weak < intros.


  Variables: X1, X2, Y1, Y2
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t X1 X2
  H2 : Y1 = X1
  H3 : Y2 = X2
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Y1 Y2

equality_for_structured_weak < case H2.


  Variables: X1, X2, Y1, Y2
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t X1 X2
  H3 : Y2 = X2
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t X1 Y2

equality_for_structured_weak < case H3.


  Variables: X1, X2, Y1, Y2
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t X1 X2
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t X1 X2

equality_for_structured_weak < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem bisim_implies_bisimWeak : 
forall P Q, bisim_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q.



  ============================
   forall P Q, bisim_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisim_implies_bisimWeak < skip.
Proof completed.

forall P, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P.



  ============================
   forall P, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P

bisimWeak_refl < skip.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem bisimWeak_sym : 
forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q P.



  ============================
   forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q P

bisimWeak_sym < skip.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem bisimWeak_trans : 
forall P Q R, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q R ->
  bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R.



  ============================
   forall P Q R, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q R ->
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R

bisimWeak_trans < skip.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem bisimWeakUpTo_sym : 
forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q P.



  ============================
   forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q P

bisimWeakUpTo_sym < skip.

Abella < Define is_sound : (proc -> proc -> proc -> proc -> prop) -> prop by 
is_sound Upto := forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to Upto P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q.

Abella < Define is_sound_fst : (proc -> proc -> proc -> proc -> prop) -> prop by 
is_sound_fst Upto := forall P Q, (exists R S, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\
  bisimWeak_up_to Upto R S /\ bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q) ->
  bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q.

Abella < Define is_sound_snd : (proc -> proc -> proc -> proc -> prop) -> prop by 
is_sound_snd Upto := forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to Upto P Q -> (exists R S,
  bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to Upto R S /\
  bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q).

Abella < Theorem bisimWeak_sound_fst : 
is_sound_fst bisim_t.



  ============================
   is_sound_fst bisim_t

bisimWeak_sound_fst < unfold.



  ============================

     bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\ bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q) ->
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

          bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M2 W) (N2 W)))
  H12 : oneWeak R A Q2
  H13 : refl_t P1 P3 Q2 Q3
  H14 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P3 Q3

   exists Q1, oneWeak Q A Q1 /\ (exists P2 Q2, refl_t P1 P2 Q1 Q2 /\

Subgoal 1:

  Variables: P, Q, R, S, A, P1, Q2, P3, Q3
  CH : forall P Q, (exists R S, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\
         bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\ bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q) ->
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q +

          (exists P3 Q3, refl_t P2 P3 Q2 Q3 /\ bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P3 Q3))
  H25 : forall X M, oneWeakb P (dn X) M -> (exists N, oneWeakb R (dn X) N /\
          (exists M2 N2, forall W, refl_t (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
          bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M2 W) (N2 W)))
  H26 : forall X M, oneWeakb P (up X) M -> (exists N, oneWeakb R (up X) N /\
          (exists M2 N2, nabla W, refl_t (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
          bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M2 W) (N2 W)))
  H27 : forall A Q2, oneWeak R A Q2 -> (exists P2, oneWeak P A P2 /\
          (exists P3 Q3, refl_t P2 P3 Q2 Q3 /\ bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P3 Q3))
  H28 : forall X N, oneWeakb R (dn X) N -> (exists M, oneWeakb P (dn X) M /\
          (exists M2 N2, forall W, refl_t (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
          bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M2 W) (N2 W)))
  H29 : forall X N, oneWeakb R (up X) N -> (exists M, oneWeakb P (up X) M /\
          (exists M2 N2, nabla W, refl_t (M W) (M2 W) (N W) (N2 W) /\
          bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M2 W) (N2 W)))
  H30 : oneWeakb P (up X) (z1\M5 z1)
  H32 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M5 n1) (N3 n1)
  H33 : bisim_up_to refl_t (N3 n1) (M3 n1)
  H34 : bisim_up_to refl_t (M2 n1) (N1 n1)
  H35 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (N3 n1) (M3 n1)
  H36 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M2 n1) (N1 n1)
  H37 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M5 n1) (M3 n1)
  H38 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (N1 n1) (M2 n1)
  H39 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (N1 n1) (N2 n1)
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t (M5 n1) (N2 n1) +

bisimWeak_sound_fst < backchain CH.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem bisimWeak_sound_snd : 
is_sound_snd bisim_t.



  ============================
   is_sound_snd bisim_t

bisimWeak_sound_snd < unfold.



  ============================
   forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q -> (exists R S,
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q)

bisimWeak_sound_snd < intros.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  ============================
   exists R S, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q

bisimWeak_sound_snd < apply bisimWeak_refl with P = P.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H2 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P
  ============================
   exists R S, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q

bisimWeak_sound_snd < apply bisimWeak_refl with P = Q.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H2 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P
  H3 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q Q
  ============================
   exists R S, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q

bisimWeak_sound_snd < exists P.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H2 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P
  H3 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q Q
  ============================
   exists S, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P S /\
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q

bisimWeak_sound_snd < exists Q.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H2 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P
  H3 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q Q
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P P /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q /\
     bisimWeak_up_to refl_t Q Q

bisimWeak_sound_snd < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem bisimWeak_sound : 
is_sound bisim_t.



  ============================
   is_sound bisim_t

bisimWeak_sound < unfold.



  ============================
   forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q -> bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisimWeak_sound < intros.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisimWeak_sound < apply bisimWeak_sound_snd.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H2 : is_sound_snd bisim_t
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisimWeak_sound < case H2.


  Variables: P, Q
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H3 : forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q -> (exists R S,
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q)
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisimWeak_sound < apply H3 to H1.


  Variables: P, Q, R, S
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H3 : forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q -> (exists R S,
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q)
  H4 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R
  H5 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S
  H6 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisimWeak_sound < apply bisimWeak_sound_fst.


  Variables: P, Q, R, S
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H3 : forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q -> (exists R S,
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q)
  H4 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R
  H5 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S
  H6 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q
  H7 : is_sound_fst bisim_t
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisimWeak_sound < case H7.


  Variables: P, Q, R, S
  H1 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q
  H3 : forall P Q, bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t P Q -> (exists R S,
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\ bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q)
  H4 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R
  H5 : bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S
  H6 : bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q
  H8 : forall P Q, (exists R S, bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P R /\
         bisimWeak_up_to bisim_t R S /\ bisimWeak_up_to refl_t S Q) ->
         bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q
  ============================
   bisimWeak_up_to refl_t P Q

bisimWeak_sound < backchain H8.
Proof completed.

Abella < Goodbye.
